said Hung Huang, a well-known social commentator based in Beijing. &quot;It was hilarious.&quot;" data-reactid="33">Viewers more used to seeing the idols play love interests in light-hearted soap operas responded to the film by projecting "modern-day romantic narratives on the founding fathers of the nation," said Hung Huang, a well-known social commentator based in Beijing. "It was hilarious."</p><p class="canvas-atom canvas-text Mb(1.0em) Mb(0)--sm Mt(0.8em)--sm" type="text" content="While China&#x27;s resurgent Communist Party once pushed its policies on an unquestioning public, it now struggles to compete for attention with the country&#x27;s booming entertainment industry and the celebrity culture it has spawned." data-reactid="34">While China's resurgent Communist Party once pushed its policies on an unquestioning public, it now struggles to compete for attention with the country's booming entertainment industry and the celebrity culture it has spawned.</p><p class="canvas-atom canvas-text Mb(1.0em) Mb(0)--sm Mt(0.8em)--sm" type="text" content="&quot;Chinese people are increasingly ignoring party propaganda and are much more interested in movie stars, who represent a new lifestyle and more exciting aspirations,&quot; said Willy Lam, an expert on Chinese politics at the Chinese University of Hong Kong." data-reactid="35">"Chinese people are increasingly ignoring party propaganda and are much more interested in movie stars, who represent a new lifestyle and more exciting aspirations," said Willy Lam, an expert on Chinese politics at the Chinese University of Hong Kong.</p><p class="canvas-atom canvas-text Mb(1.0em) Mb(0)--sm Mt(0.8em)--sm" type="text" content="President Xi Jinping, who will cement his authority with his expected endorsement to a second five-year term at this week&#x27;s national party congress, has placed a priority on stamping out too much Western influence in Chinese society in part so the party can dictate the values the youth should embrace." data-reactid="36">President Xi Jinping, who will cement his authority with his expected endorsement to a second five-year term at this week's national party congress, has placed a priority on stamping out too much Western influence in Chinese society in part so the party can dictate the values the youth should embrace.</p><p class="canvas-atom canvas-text Mb(1.0em) Mb(0)--sm Mt(0.8em)--sm" type="text" content="Authorities have responded by targeting everything from gossip websites to soap opera story lines to celebrity salaries. Instead of selfish, rich stars, the state is promoting performers who are all about patriotism, purity and other values that support the party&#x27;s legitimacy." data-reactid="37">Authorities have responded by targeting everything from gossip websites to soap opera story lines to celebrity salaries. Instead of selfish, rich stars, the state is promoting performers who are all about patriotism, purity and other values that support the party's legitimacy.</p><p class="canvas-atom canvas-text Mb(1.0em) Mb(0)--sm Mt(0.8em)--sm" type="text" content="The results have at best been mixed and at worst ham-fisted and out of touch." data-reactid="38">The results have at best been mixed and at worst ham-fisted and out of touch.</p><p class="canvas-atom canvas-text Mb(1.0em) Mb(0)--sm Mt(0.8em)--sm" type="text" content="One problem is that the party&#x27;s values often clash with what young Chinese want to watch, according to Hung. Among the more popular shows watched by Chinese youth are those that center on palace intrigue, martial arts fantasies, high school romances or single, independent women." data-reactid="39">One problem is that the party's values often clash with what young Chinese want to watch, according to Hung. Among the more popular shows watched by Chinese youth are those that center on palace intrigue, martial arts fantasies, high school romances or single, independent women.</p><p class="canvas-atom canvas-text Mb(1.0em) Mb(0)--sm Mt(0.8em)--sm" type="text" content="&quot;While the government could once dictate to young people what they should value and how they should lead their lives, they find themselves completely without the tools to do that now,&quot; But it has gained new traction since Xi came to power in 2012 and officials began a wide-ranging crackdown on perceived societal ills from corruption to dissent to — now — entertainment.","length":341,"tagName":"p"},{"type":"text","content":"\"Xi Jinping has been advocating a revision to traditional, Confucian moral standards,\" Lam said. \"The definition of what is vulgar or morally problematic has been inflated and expanded so that it has become all-encompassing.\"","length":225,"tagName":"p"},{"type":"text","content":"Shows about the pursuit of great wealth and luxury that used to be tolerated under Xi's predecessor, aren't anymore.","length":116,"tagName":"p"},{"type":"text","content":"The government has demanded that broadcasters \"resist celebrity worship\" and limit the air time dedicated to film and TV stars.","length":127,"tagName":"p"},{"type":"text","content":"\"The party does not want these entertainment programs to compete with news programs and 'morality shows,'\" said Jian Xu, a Chinese media research fellow at Deakin University in Melbourne, Australia.","length":198,"tagName":"p"},{"type":"text","content":"One example of a state-approved show is \"Touching China,\" which honors people who have \"touched the nation with their tenacity, bravery and wisdom.\"","length":148,"tagName":"p"},{"type":"text","content":"The government has also tried to shape some celebrities into party-sanctioned role models.","length":90,"tagName":"p"},{"type":"text","content":"Thanks to their wholesome image and uplifting, patriotic lyrics, the TFboys, China's first home-grown boy band, have risen to fame because of \"political opportunities\" they've been given, Xu said.
